     1 import { createContext, useContext, useEffect, useState, useCallback, type ReactNode } from 'react';
     2 import { supabase } from '@/db/supabase';
     3 import type { User } from '@supabase/supabase-js';
     4 import type { PermissionKey, Permissions, Profile, Store } from '@/types/types';
     5 
     6 export async function getProfile(userId: string): Promise<Profile | null> {
     7   const { data, error } = await supabase
     8     .from('profiles')
     9     .select('*, custom_role:roles(*)')
    10     .eq('id', userId)
    11     .maybeSingle();
    12   if (error) {
    13     console.error('ดึงข้อมูลผู้ใช้ไม่สำเร็จ:', error);
    14     return null;
    15   }
    16   return data;
    17 }
    18 
    19 interface AuthContextType {
    20   user: User | null;
    21   profile: Profile | null;
    22   store: Store | null;
    23   permissions: Permissions;
    24   loading: boolean;
    25   isAdmin: boolean;
    26   isStoreOwner: boolean;
    27   isSuperAdmin: boolean;
    28   can: (permission: PermissionKey) => boolean;
    29   signInWithUsername: (username: string, password: string) => Promise<{ error: Error | null; blocked?: boolean; storeClosed?: boolean }>;
    30   signUpWithUsername: (username: string, password: string, fullName?: string, storeId?: string, role?: string) => Promise<{ error: Error | null }>;
    31   signOut: () => Promise<void>;
    32   refreshProfile: () => Promise<void>;
    33 }
    34 
    35 const AuthContext = createContext<AuthContextType | undefined>(undefined);
    36 
    37 /** รวม permissions จาก custom_role (ถ้ามี) หรือใช้ค่า default ตาม role */
    38 function resolvePermissions(profile: Profile | null): Permissions {
    39   if (!profile) return {};
    40   const allKeys: PermissionKey[] = [
    41     'view_dashboard','view_reports','view_profit','manage_products','manage_inventory',
    42     'manage_users','manage_settings','process_sales','void_transactions','view_transactions',
    43     'view_all_transactions','manage_categories','view_cost','manage_roles',
    44     'view_audit_log','view_fraud_alerts','issue_warnings',
    45   ];
    46   // super_admin + store_owner + admin มีสิทธิ์ทุกอย่าง
    47   if (['super_admin','store_owner','admin'].includes(profile.role)) {
    48     const all: Permissions = {};
    49     allKeys.forEach(k => { all[k] = true; });
    50     return all;
    51   }
    52   if (profile.custom_role?.permissions) return profile.custom_role.permissions;
    53   return { process_sales: true, view_transactions: true };
    54 }
    55 
    56 export function AuthProvider({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) {
    57   const [user, setUser] = useState<User | null>(null);
    58   const [profile, setProfile] = useState<Profile | null>(null);
    59   const [store, setStore] = useState<Store | null>(null);
    60   const [permissions, setPermissions] = useState<Permissions>({});
    61   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
    62 
    63   /** โหลดข้อมูลร้านใน background — ไม่บล็อก loading */
    64   const loadStore = useCallback(async (storeId: string | null | undefined) => {
    65     if (!storeId) { setStore(null); return; }
    66     const { data } = await supabase
    67       .from('stores')
    68       .select('*')
    69       .eq('id', storeId)
    70       .maybeSingle();
    71     setStore(data ?? null);
    72   }, []);
    73 
    74   const applyProfile = useCallback((p: Profile | null) => {
    75     setProfile(p);
    76     setPermissions(resolvePermissions(p));
    77     // โหลดร้านแบบ background (ไม่ await ที่นี่)
    78     if (p?.store_id && p.role !== 'super_admin') {
    79       loadStore(p.store_id);
    80     } else {
    81       setStore(null);
    82     }
    83   }, [loadStore]);
    84 
    85   const refreshProfile = useCallback(async () => {
    86     if (!user) { applyProfile(null); return; }
    87     const profileData = await getProfile(user.id);
    88     applyProfile(profileData);
    89   }, [user, applyProfile]);
    90 
    91   useEffect(() => {
    92     // โหลด session ครั้งแรก — set loading=false ทันทีที่ profile พร้อม
    93     supabase.auth.getSession()
    94       .then(async ({ data: { session } }) => {
    95         setUser(session?.user ?? null);
    96         if (session?.user) {
    97           const p = await getProfile(session.user.id);
    98           applyProfile(p);
    99         }
   100       })
   101       .catch(console.error)
   102       .finally(() => setLoading(false));
   103 
   104     // onAuthStateChange จะยิง INITIAL_SESSION ซ้ำ — ข้ามรอบแรก
   105     const { data: { subscription } } = supabase.auth.onAuthStateChange(async (event, session) => {
   106       // ข้าม INITIAL_SESSION เพราะ getSession จัดการแล้ว
   107       if (event === 'INITIAL_SESSION') return;
   108       setUser(session?.user ?? null);
   109       if (session?.user) {
   110         const p = await getProfile(session.user.id);
   111         applyProfile(p);
   112       } else {
   113         applyProfile(null);
   114       }
   115     });
   116 
   117     return () => subscription.unsubscribe();
   118   }, [applyProfile]);
   119 
   120   const signInWithUsername = async (username: string, password: string) => {
   121     try {
   122       const email = `${username}@miaoda.com`;
   123       const { error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({ email, password });
   124       if (error) throw error;
   125 
   126       // ดึงข้อมูลโปรไฟล์พร้อม store_id
   127       const { data: profileData } = await supabase
   128         .from('profiles')
   129         .select('warning_status, role, store_id')
   130         .eq('username', username)
   131         .maybeSingle();
   132 
   133       // บล็อคใบแดง
   134       if (profileData?.warning_status === 'red_card') {
   135         await supabase.auth.signOut();
   136         return { error: new Error('ACCOUNT_SUSPENDED'), blocked: true };
   137       }
   138 
   139       // ตรวจสอบว่าร้านยังเปิดอยู่ (เฉพาะ non-super_admin)
   140       if (profileData?.role !== 'super_admin' && profileData?.store_id) {
   141         const { data: storeData } = await supabase
   142           .from('stores')
   143           .select('is_active')
   144           .eq('id', profileData.store_id)
   145           .maybeSingle();
   146         if (storeData && !storeData.is_active) {
   147           await supabase.auth.signOut();
   148           return { error: new Error('STORE_CLOSED'), storeClosed: true };
   149         }
   150       }
   151 
   152       return { error: null };
   153     } catch (error) {
   154       return { error: error as Error };
   155     }
   156   };
   157 
   158   const signUpWithUsername = async (
   159     username: string,
   160     password: string,
   161     fullName?: string,
   162     storeId?: string,
   163     role: string = 'cashier',
   164   ) => {
   165     try {
   166       const email = `${username}@miaoda.com`;
   167       const { error } = await supabase.auth.signUp({
   168         email,
   169         password,
   170         options: { data: { username, full_name: fullName || username, store_id: storeId, role } },
   171       });
   172       if (error) throw error;
   173       return { error: null };
   174     } catch (error) {
   175       return { error: error as Error };
   176     }
   177   };
   178 
   179   const signOut = async () => {
   180     await supabase.auth.signOut();
   181     setUser(null);
   182     await applyProfile(null);
   183   };
   184 
   185   const isAdmin = ['admin','store_owner','super_admin'].includes(profile?.role ?? '');
   186   const isStoreOwner = profile?.role === 'store_owner' || profile?.role === 'admin';
   187   const isSuperAdmin = profile?.role === 'super_admin';
   188 
   189   const can = useCallback((permission: PermissionKey): boolean => {
   190     if (isAdmin) return true;
   191     return permissions[permission] === true;
   192   }, [isAdmin, permissions]);
   193 
   194   return (
   195     <AuthContext.Provider value={{
   196       user, profile, store, permissions, loading,
   197       isAdmin, isStoreOwner, isSuperAdmin,
   198       can, signInWithUsername, signUpWithUsername, signOut, refreshProfile,
   199     }}>
   200       {children}
   201     </AuthContext.Provider>
   202   );
   203 }
   204 
   205 export function useAuth() {
   206   const context = useContext(AuthContext);
   207   if (context === undefined) {
   208     // Return safe defaults during HMR / Fast Refresh re-evaluation
   209     // instead of throwing — prevents crash when component is briefly
   210     // rendered outside the provider tree during hot reload.
   211     return {
   212       user: null, profile: null, store: null, permissions: {},
   213       loading: true, isAdmin: false, isStoreOwner: false, isSuperAdmin: false,
   214       can: () => false,
   215       signInWithUsername: async () => ({ error: new Error('No AuthProvider') }),
   216       signUpWithUsername: async () => ({ error: new Error('No AuthProvider') }),
   217       signOut: async () => {},
   218       refreshProfile: async () => {},
   219     } as AuthContextType;
   220   }
   221   return context;
   222 }

     7 // Smart root redirect: admin/store_owner/super_admin → /dashboard, cashier → /pos
     8 function RootRedirect() {
     9   const { user, profile, loading } = useAuth();
    10   if (loading) {
    11     return (
    12       <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-background">
    13         <div className="w-8 h-8 rounded-full border-2 border-primary border-t-transparent animate-spin" />

    16   }

    20   return <Navigate to="/pos" replace />;
    21 }

     2 import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';

    17 const loginSchema = z.object({
    18   username: z.string().min(1).regex(/^[a-zA-Z0-9_]+$/),
    19   password: z.string().min(6),
    20   agree: z.boolean().refine(v => v),
    21 });
    22 
    23 type LoginForm = z.infer<typeof loginSchema>;
    24 
    25 export default function LoginPage() {
    26   const navigate = useNavigate();
    27   const { signInWithUsername } = useAuth();
    28   const { t } = useTranslation();
    29   const [showPassword, setShowPassword] = useState(false);
    30   const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
    31   const [storeName, setStoreName] = useState<string | null>(null);
    32   const [logoUrl, setLogoUrl] = useState<string | null>(null);
    33 
    34   useEffect(() => {
    35     supabase.from('store_settings').select('store_name, logo_url').maybeSingle().then(({ data }) => {
    36       if (data) { setStoreName(data.store_name ?? null); setLogoUrl((data as any).logo_url ?? null); }
    37     });
    38   }, []);
    39 
    40   const form = useForm<LoginForm>({
    41     resolver: zodResolver(loginSchema),
    42     defaultValues: { username: '', password: '', agree: false },
    43   });
    44 
    45   const onSubmit = async (data: LoginForm) => {
    46     setIsLoading(true);
    47     const { error, blocked, storeClosed } = await signInWithUsername(data.username, data.password);
    48     setIsLoading(false);
    49     if (error) {
    50       if (blocked) {
    51         toast.error(t('login.accountSuspended'), { duration: 6000 });
    52       } else if (storeClosed) {
    53         toast.error(t('login.storeClosed'), { duration: 6000 });
    54       } else {
    55         toast.error(t('login.invalidCredentials'));
    56       }
    57       if (!blocked && !storeClosed) {
    58         await supabase.from('failed_logins').insert({ username: data.username });
    59         await supabase.from('audit_logs').insert({
    60           user_id: null,
    61           username: data.username,
    62           action: 'failed_login',
    63           entity_type: 'auth',
    64           entity_id: null,
    65           details: {},
    66           severity: 'warning',
    67         });
    68         await supabase.rpc('check_brute_force', { p_username: data.username });
    69       }
    70     } else {
    71       toast.success(t('login.loginSuccess'));
    72       const { data: profileData } = await supabase
    73         .from('profiles')
    74         .select('id, username')
    75         .eq('username', data.username)
    76         .maybeSingle();
    77       if (profileData) {
    78         await supabase.from('audit_logs').insert({
    79           user_id: profileData.id,
    80           username: profileData.username,
    81           action: 'login',
    82           entity_type: 'auth',
    83           entity_id: null,
    84           details: {},
    85           severity: 'info',
    86         });
    87       }
    88       navigate('/');
    89     }
    90   };
    91 
    92   return (
    93     <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-background p-4">
    94       {/* Language switcher — top right */}
    95       <div className="fixed top-4 right-4 z-50">
    96         <LanguageSwitcher />
    97       </div>
    98 
    99       <div className="w-full max-w-sm">
   100         {/* Logo */}
   101         <div className="flex flex-col items-center mb-8">
   102           {logoUrl ? (
   103             <img src={logoUrl} alt="store logo" className="w-16 h-16 rounded-2xl object-contain mb-4 shadow-md bg-card border border-border" />
   104           ) : (
   105             <div className="w-16 h-16 rounded-2xl bg-primary flex items-center justify-center mb-4 shadow-md">
   106               <ShoppingCart className="w-8 h-8 text-primary-foreground" />
   107             </div>
   108           )}
   109           <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-foreground text-balance">
   110             {storeName || t('login.systemName')}
   111           </h1>
   112           <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mt-1">POS System</p>
   113         </div>
   114 
   115         {/* Card */}
   116         <div className="bg-card rounded-xl border border-border shadow-md p-6">
   117           <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-foreground mb-5">{t('login.title')}</h2>
   118           <Form {...form}>
   119             <form onSubmit={form.handleSubmit(onSubmit)} className="space-y-4">
   120               <FormField
   121                 control={form.control}
   122                 name="username"

The `signInWithUsername` function itself doesn\'t update React state - it just calls Supabase. The `onAuthStateChange` handler updates state.\n\nSo when `signInWithUsername` returns `{ error: null }` and LoginPage calls `navigate(\'/\')`:\n- `user` in AuthContext might still be null (if SIGNED_IN handler hasn\'t run setUser yet)\n- OR `user` is set but `profile` is still null (getProfile is pending)\n\nIf `user=null` when navigate(\'/\') runs → `RootRedirect` redirects to `/login` → we\'re back at login page → INFINITE LOOP / appears to hang!\n\nThis is the real bug. The race condition:\n1. LoginPage calls signInWithUsername → returns { error: null }\n2. LoginPage calls navigate(\'/\')\n3. RootRedirect checks user → still null (SIGNED_IN hasn\'t updated state yet) OR profile is null\n4. Navigate to /login again\n5. User thinks login is hanging/looping\n\nThe fix: In LoginPage.onSubmit, instead of calling navigate(\'/\') immediately after signInWithUsername returns, we should WAIT for the auth state to update. \n\nOr better: let `onAuthStateChange` handle the navigation.      6 export async function getProfile(userId: string): Promise<Profile | null> {
     7   const { data, error } = await supabase
     8     .from('profiles')
     9     .select('*, custom_role:roles(*)')
    10     .eq('id', userId)
    11     .maybeSingle();
    12   if (error) {
    13     console.error('ดึงข้อมูลผู้ใช้ไม่สำเร็จ:', error);
    14     return null;
    15   }
    16   return data;
    17 }

    19 interface AuthContextType {
    20   user: User | null;
    21   profile: Profile | null;
    22   store: Store | null;
    23   permissions: Permissions;
    24   loading: boolean;
    25   isAdmin: boolean;
    26   isStoreOwner: boolean;
    27   isSuperAdmin: boolean;

    30   signUpWithUsername: (username: string, password: string, fullName?: string, storeId?: string, role?: string) => Promise<{ error: Error | null }>;
    31   signOut: () => Promise<void>;
    32   refreshProfile: () => Promise<void>;

    35 const AuthContext = createContext<AuthContextType | undefined>(undefined);

    37 /** รวม permissions จาก custom_role (ถ้ามี) หรือใช้ค่า default ตาม role */
    38 function resolvePermissions(profile: Profile | null): Permissions {
    39   if (!profile) return {};
    40   const allKeys: PermissionKey[] = [
    41     'view_dashboard','view_reports','view_profit','manage_products','manage_inventory',
    42     'manage_users','manage_settings','process_sales','void_transactions','view_transactions',
    43     'view_all_transactions','manage_categories','view_cost','manage_roles',
    44     'view_audit_log','view_fraud_alerts','issue_warnings',
    45   ];
    46   // super_admin + store_owner + admin มีสิทธิ์ทุกอย่าง
    47   if (['super_admin','store_owner','admin'].includes(profile.role)) {
    48     const all: Permissions = {};
    49     allKeys.forEach(k => { all[k] = true; });
    50     return all;
    51   }
    52   if (profile.custom_role?.permissions) return profile.custom_role.permissions;
    53   return { process_sales: true, view_transactions: true };
    54 }
    55 
    56 export function AuthProvider({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) {
    57   const [user, setUser] = useState<User | null>(null);
    58   const [profile, setProfile] = useState<Profile | null>(null);
    59   const [store, setStore] = useState<Store | null>(null);
    60   const [permissions, setPermissions] = useState<Permissions>({});
    61   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
    62 
    63   /** โหลดข้อมูลร้านใน background — ไม่บล็อก loading */
    64   const loadStore = useCallback(async (storeId: string | null | undefined) => {
    65     if (!storeId) { setStore(null); return; }
    66     const { data } = await supabase
    67       .from('stores')
    68       .select('*')
    69       .eq('id', storeId)
    70       .maybeSingle();
    71     setStore(data ?? null);
    72   }, []);
    73 
    74   const applyProfile = useCallback((p: Profile | null) => {
    75     setProfile(p);
    76     setPermissions(resolvePermissions(p));
    77     // โหลดร้านแบบ background (ไม่ await ที่นี่)
    78     if (p?.store_id && p.role !== 'super_admin') {
    79       loadStore(p.store_id);
    80     } else {
    81       setStore(null);
    82     }
    83   }, [loadStore]);
    84 
    85   const refreshProfile = useCallback(async () => {
    86     if (!user) { applyProfile(null); return; }
    87     const profileData = await getProfile(user.id);
    88     applyProfile(profileData);
    89   }, [user, applyProfile]);
    90 
    91   useEffect(() => {
    92     // ใช้ onAuthStateChange เป็น single source of truth
    93     // INITIAL_SESSION จะยิงทันทีพร้อม session จริง (รวมถึงกรณี token หมดอายุ)
    94     const { data: { subscription } } = supabase.auth.onAuthStateChange(async (event, session) => {
    95       if (event === 'SIGNED_OUT' || (!session && event !== 'INITIAL_SESSION')) {
    96         // token หมดอายุ หรือ logout — ล้าง state และกลับหน้า login
    97         setUser(null);
    98         applyProfile(null);
    99         setLoading(false);
   100         return;
   101       }
   102       setUser(session?.user ?? null);
   103       if (session?.user) {
   104         const p = await getProfile(session.user.id);
   105         applyProfile(p);
   106       } else {
   107         applyProfile(null);
   108       }
   109       // loading=false หลังจาก INITIAL_SESSION หรือ SIGNED_IN ประมวลผลเสร็จ
   110       if (event === 'INITIAL_SESSION' || event === 'SIGNED_IN') {
   111         setLoading(false);
   112       }
   113     });
   114 
   115     // fallback: ถ้า INITIAL_SESSION ไม่ยิงภายใน 5 วินาที ให้ยกเลิก loading
   116     const fallback = setTimeout(() => setLoading(false), 5000);
   117 
   118     return () => {
   119       subscription.unsubscribe();
   120       clearTimeout(fallback);
   121     };
   122   }, [applyProfile]);
   123 
   124   const signInWithUsername = async (username: string, password: string) => {
   125     try {
   126       const email = `${username}@miaoda.com`;
   127       const { error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({ email, password });
   128       if (error) throw error;
   129 
   130       // ดึงข้อมูลโปรไฟล์พร้อม store_id
   131       const { data: profileData } = await supabase
   132         .from('profiles')
   133         .select('warning_status, role, store_id')
   134         .eq('username', username)
   135         .maybeSingle();
   136 
   137       // บล็อคใบแดง
   138       if (profileData?.warning_status === 'red_card') {
   139         await supabase.auth.signOut();
   140         return { error: new Error('ACCOUNT_SUSPENDED'), blocked: true };
   141       }
   142 
   143       // ตรวจสอบว่าร้านยังเปิดอยู่ (เฉพาะ non-super_admin)
   144       if (profileData?.role !== 'super_admin' && profileData?.store_id) {
   145         const { data: storeData } = await supabase
   146           .from('stores')
   147           .select('is_active')
   148           .eq('id', profileData.store_id)
   149           .maybeSingle();
   150         if (storeData && !storeData.is_active) {
   151           await supabase.auth.signOut();
   152           return { error: new Error('STORE_CLOSED'), storeClosed: true };
   153         }
   154       }
   155 
   156       return { error: null };
   157     } catch (error) {
   158       return { error: error as Error };
   159     }
   160   };
   161 
   162   const signUpWithUsername = async (
   163     username: string,
   164     password: string,
   165     fullName?: string,
   166     storeId?: string,
   167     role: string = 'cashier',
   168   ) => {
   169     try {
   170       const email = `${username}@miaoda.com`;
   171       const { error } = await supabase.auth.signUp({
   172         email,
   173         password,
   174         options: { data: { username, full_name: fullName || username, store_id: storeId, role } },
   175       });
   176       if (error) throw error;
   177       return { error: null };
   178     } catch (error) {
   179       return { error: error as Error };
   180     }
   181   };
   182 
   183   const signOut = async () => {
   184     await supabase.auth.signOut();
   185     setUser(null);
   186     await applyProfile(null);
   187   };
   188 
   189   const isAdmin = ['admin','store_owner','super_admin'].includes(profile?.role ?? '');
   190   const isStoreOwner = profile?.role === 'store_owner' || profile?.role === 'admin';
   191   const isSuperAdmin = profile?.role === 'super_admin';
   192 
   193   const can = useCallback((permission: PermissionKey): boolean => {
   194     if (isAdmin) return true;
   195     return permissions[permission] === true;
   196   }, [isAdmin, permissions]);
   197 
   198   return (
   199     <AuthContext.Provider value={{
   200       user, profile, store, permissions, loading,
   201       isAdmin, isStoreOwner, isSuperAdmin,
   202       can, signInWithUsername, signUpWithUsername, signOut, refreshProfile,
   203     }}>
   204       {children}
   205     </AuthContext.Provider>
   206   );
   207 }
   208 
   209 export function useAuth() {
   210   const context = useContext(AuthContext);
   211   if (context === undefined) {
   212     // Return safe defaults during HMR / Fast Refresh re-evaluation
   213     // instead of throwing — prevents crash when component is briefly
   214     // rendered outside the provider tree during hot reload.
   215     return {
   216       user: null, profile: null, store: null, permissions: {},
   217       loading: true, isAdmin: false, isStoreOwner: false, isSuperAdmin: false,
   218       can: () => false,
   219       signInWithUsername: async () => ({ error: new Error('No AuthProvider') }),
   220       signUpWithUsername: async () => ({ error: new Error('No AuthProvider') }),
   221       signOut: async () => {},
   222       refreshProfile: async () => {},
   223     } as AuthContextType;
   224   }
   225   return context;
   226 }

This triggers `onAuthStateChange(SIGNED_IN)` **asynchronously** (it\'s event-based, not synchronous)\n4. `signInWithUsername` continues and returns `{ error: null }` to LoginPage\n5. LoginPage calls `navigate(\'/\')` \n6. `RootRedirect` renders:\n   - `loading = false` (from INITIAL_SESSION earlier)\n   - `user = null` (SIGNED_IN handler hasn\'t fired yet OR is still awaiting `getProfile()`)\n   - So it redirects to `/login` again!\n7. User sees login page again → appears to "hang" or loop\n\n**Fix strategy:**\n\nThe most reliable fix: In `signInWithUsername`, after `signInWithPassword` succeeds, **immediately update the user state synchronously** before returning. This ensures state is set before `navigate(\'/\')` is called.\n\nAdd after `signInWithPassword` succeeds:\n```js\nconst { data: { session }, error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithPassword(...)\n// Immediately set user in state so navigate(\'/\') works correctly\nif (session?.user) {\n  setUser(session.user);\n  const p = await getProfile(session.user.id);\n  applyProfile(p);\n}\n```\n\nThis way, by the time `signInWithUsername` returns and LoginPage calls `navigate(\'/\')`, both `user` and `profile` are already set in React state. The `onAuthStateChange(SIGNED_IN)` will fire later but just re-sets the same values (no-op effectively).\n\nI also need to handle the case where the user has `red_card` or `storeClosed` - in those cases we call `supabase.auth.signOut()` which triggers `SIGNED_OUT` → clears state → back to login (correct behavior).\n\nAlso need to remove the duplicate loading=false call since loading is already false by this point (set during INITIAL_SESSION). Or keep it just as a safety net.\n\nLet me rewrite `signInWithUsername` to eagerly update state.\n', action=<ActionType.THINK: 'think'>)

New String: ```
  const signInWithUsername = async (username: string, password: string) => {
    try {
      const email = `${username}@miaoda.com`;
      const { data: { session }, error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({ email, password });
      if (error) throw error;

      // ดึงข้อมูลโปรไฟล์พร้อม store_id
      const { data: profileData } = await supabase
        .from('profiles')
        .select('*, custom_role:roles(*), warning_status, role, store_id')
        .eq('username', username)
        .maybeSingle();

      // บล็อคใบแดง
      if (profileData?.warning_status === 'red_card') {
        await supabase.auth.signOut();
        setUser(null);
        applyProfile(null);
        return { error: new Error('ACCOUNT_SUSPENDED'), blocked: true };
      }

      // ตรวจสอบว่าร้านยังเปิดอยู่ (เฉพาะ non-super_admin)
      if (profileData?.role !== 'super_admin' && profileData?.store_id) {
        const { data: storeData } = await supabase
          .from('stores')
          .select('is_active')
          .eq('id', profileData.store_id)
          .maybeSingle();
        if (storeData && !storeData.is_active) {
          await supabase.auth.signOut();
          setUser(null);
          applyProfile(null);
          return { error: new Error('STORE_CLOSED'), storeClosed: true };
        }
      }

      // ✅ อัปเดต state ทันทีก่อน return — ป้องกัน race condition กับ navigate('/')
      // onAuthStateChange(SIGNED_IN) จะยิงทีหลัง แต่ค่าจะเหมือนกัน
      if (session?.user) {
        setUser(session.user);
        applyProfile(profileData as Profile | null);
        setLoading(false);
      }

      return { error: null };
    } catch (error) {
      return { error: error as Error };
    }
  };
```

```
  useEffect(() => {
    // ใช้ onAuthStateChange เป็น single source of truth สำหรับ session ครั้งแรก
    // SIGNED_IN จะถูกจัดการใน signInWithUsername โดยตรงเพื่อป้องกัน race condition
```

    27   isSuperAdmin: boolean;
    28   can: (permission: PermissionKey) => boolean;
    29   signInWithUsername: (username: string, password: string) => Promise<{ error: Error | null; blocked?: boolean; storeClosed?: boolean }>;
    30   signUpWithUsername: (username: string, password: string, fullName?: string, storeId?: string, role?: string) => Promise<{ error: Error | null }>;
    31   signOut: () => Promise<void>;
    32   refreshProfile: () => Promise<void>;
    33 }
    34 
    35 const AuthContext = createContext<AuthContextType | undefined>(undefined);
    36 
    37 /** รวม permissions จาก custom_role (ถ้ามี) หรือใช้ค่า default ตาม role */
    38 function resolvePermissions(profile: Profile | null): Permissions {
    39   if (!profile) return {};
    40   const allKeys: PermissionKey[] = [
    41     'view_dashboard','view_reports','view_profit','manage_products','manage_inventory',
    42     'manage_users','manage_settings','process_sales','void_transactions','view_transactions',
    43     'view_all_transactions','manage_categories','view_cost','manage_roles',
    44     'view_audit_log','view_fraud_alerts','issue_warnings',
    45   ];
    46   // super_admin + store_owner + admin มีสิทธิ์ทุกอย่าง
    47   if (['super_admin','store_owner','admin'].includes(profile.role)) {
    48     const all: Permissions = {};
    49     allKeys.forEach(k => { all[k] = true; });
    50     return all;
    51   }
    52   if (profile.custom_role?.permissions) return profile.custom_role.permissions;
    53   return { process_sales: true, view_transactions: true };
    54 }
    55 
    56 export function AuthProvider({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) {
    57   const [user, setUser] = useState<User | null>(null);
    58   const [profile, setProfile] = useState<Profile | null>(null);
    59   const [store, setStore] = useState<Store | null>(null);
    60   const [permissions, setPermissions] = useState<Permissions>({});
    61   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
    62 
    63   /** โหลดข้อมูลร้านใน background — ไม่บล็อก loading */
    64   const loadStore = useCallback(async (storeId: string | null | undefined) => {
    65     if (!storeId) { setStore(null); return; }
    66     const { data } = await supabase
    67       .from('stores')
    68       .select('*')
    69       .eq('id', storeId)
    70       .maybeSingle();
    71     setStore(data ?? null);
    72   }, []);
    73 
    74   const applyProfile = useCallback((p: Profile | null) => {
    75     setProfile(p);
    76     setPermissions(resolvePermissions(p));
    77     // โหลดร้านแบบ background (ไม่ await ที่นี่)
    78     if (p?.store_id && p.role !== 'super_admin') {
    79       loadStore(p.store_id);
    80     } else {
    81       setStore(null);
    82     }
    83   }, [loadStore]);
    84 
    85   const refreshProfile = useCallback(async () => {
    86     if (!user) { applyProfile(null); return; }
    87     const profileData = await getProfile(user.id);
    88     applyProfile(profileData);
    89   }, [user, applyProfile]);
    90 
    91   useEffect(() => {
    92     // ใช้ onAuthStateChange เป็น single source of truth สำหรับ session ครั้งแรก
    93     // SIGNED_IN จะถูกจัดการใน signInWithUsername โดยตรงเพื่อป้องกัน race condition
    94     const { data: { subscription } } = supabase.auth.onAuthStateChange(async (event, session) => {
    95       if (event === 'SIGNED_OUT') {
    96         // logout หรือ token หมดอายุ — ล้าง state กลับหน้า login
    97         setUser(null);
    98         applyProfile(null);
    99         setLoading(false);
   100         return;
   101       }
   102       if (event === 'INITIAL_SESSION') {
   103         // โหลด session ครั้งแรกตอนเปิดแอป
   104         if (session?.user) {
   105           setUser(session.user);
   106           const p = await getProfile(session.user.id);
   107           applyProfile(p);
   108         } else {
   109           setUser(null);
   110           applyProfile(null);
   111         }
   112         setLoading(false);
   113         return;
   114       }
   115       if (event === 'TOKEN_REFRESHED' && session?.user) {
   116         // token ต่ออายุสำเร็จ — อัปเดต user object ใหม่
   117         setUser(session.user);
   118       }
   119     });
   120 
   121     // fallback: ถ้า INITIAL_SESSION ไม่ยิงภายใน 5 วินาที ให้ยกเลิก loading
   122     const fallback = setTimeout(() => setLoading(false), 5000);
   123 
   124     return () => {
   125       subscription.unsubscribe();
   126       clearTimeout(fallback);
   127     };
   128   }, [applyProfile]);
   129 
   130   const signInWithUsername = async (username: string, password: string) => {
   131     try {
   132       const email = `${username}@miaoda.com`;
   133       const { data: { session }, error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({ email, password });
   134       if (error) throw error;
   135 
   136       // ดึงข้อมูลโปรไฟล์พร้อม store_id
   137       const { data: profileData } = await supabase
   138         .from('profiles')
   139         .select('*, custom_role:roles(*), warning_status, role, store_id')
   140         .eq('username', username)
   141         .maybeSingle();
   142 
   143       // บล็อคใบแดง
   144       if (profileData?.warning_status === 'red_card') {
   145         await supabase.auth.signOut();
   146         setUser(null);
   147         applyProfile(null);
   148         return { error: new Error('ACCOUNT_SUSPENDED'), blocked: true };
   149       }
   150 
   151       // ตรวจสอบว่าร้านยังเปิดอยู่ (เฉพาะ non-super_admin)
   152       if (profileData?.role !== 'super_admin' && profileData?.store_id) {
   153         const { data: storeData } = await supabase
   154           .from('stores')
   155           .select('is_active')
   156           .eq('id', profileData.store_id)
   157           .maybeSingle();
   158         if (storeData && !storeData.is_active) {
   159           await supabase.auth.signOut();
   160           setUser(null);
   161           applyProfile(null);
   162           return { error: new Error('STORE_CLOSED'), storeClosed: true };
   163         }
   164       }
   165 
   166       // ✅ อัปเดต state ทันทีก่อน return — ป้องกัน race condition กับ navigate('/')
   167       // onAuthStateChange(SIGNED_IN) จะยิงทีหลัง แต่ค่าจะเหมือนกัน
   168       if (session?.user) {
   169         setUser(session.user);
   170         applyProfile(profileData as Profile | null);
   171         setLoading(false);
   172       }
   173 
   174       return { error: null };
   175     } catch (error) {
   176       return { error: error as Error };
   177     }
   178   };
   179 
   180   const signUpWithUsername = async (
   181     username: string,
   182     password: string,
   183     fullName?: string,
   184     storeId?: string,
   185     role: string = 'cashier',
   186   ) => {
   187     try {
   188       const email = `${username}@miaoda.com`;
   189       const { error } = await supabase.auth.signUp({
   190         email,
   191         password,
   192         options: { data: { username, full_name: fullName || username, store_id: storeId, role } },
   193       });
   194       if (error) throw error;
   195       return { error: null };
   196     } catch (error) {
   197       return { error: error as Error };
   198     }
   199   };
   200 
   201   const signOut = async () => {
   202     await supabase.auth.signOut();
   203     setUser(null);
   204     await applyProfile(null);
   205   };
   206 
   207   const isAdmin = ['admin','store_owner','super_admin'].includes(profile?.role ?? '');
   208   const isStoreOwner = profile?.role === 'store_owner' || profile?.role === 'admin';
   209   const isSuperAdmin = profile?.role === 'super_admin';
   210 
   211   const can = useCallback((permission: PermissionKey): boolean => {
   212     if (isAdmin) return true;
   213     return permissions[permission] === true;
   214   }, [isAdmin, permissions]);
   215 
   216   return (
   217     <AuthContext.Provider value={{
   218       user, profile, store, permissions, loading,
   219       isAdmin, isStoreOwner, isSuperAdmin,
   220       can, signInWithUsername, signUpWithUsername, signOut, refreshProfile,
   221     }}>
   222       {children}
   223     </AuthContext.Provider>
   224   );
   225 }
   226 
   227 export function useAuth() {
   228   const context = useContext(AuthContext);
   229   if (context === undefined) {
   230     // Return safe defaults during HMR / Fast Refresh re-evaluation
   231     // instead of throwing — prevents crash when component is briefly
   232     // rendered outside the provider tree during hot reload.
   233     return {
   234       user: null, profile: null, store: null, permissions: {},
   235       loading: true, isAdmin: false, isStoreOwner: false, isSuperAdmin: false,
   236       can: () => false,
   237       signInWithUsername: async () => ({ error: new Error('No AuthProvider') }),
   238       signUpWithUsername: async () => ({ error: new Error('No AuthProvider') }),
   239       signOut: async () => {},
   240       refreshProfile: async () => {},
   241     } as AuthContextType;
   242   }
   243   return context;
   244 }

    67   });

    69   const getRoleName = () => {
    70     if (profile?.role === 'super_admin') return t('roleLabel.super_admin');

   144 export default function RolesPage() {

    12 // -------- Helpers --------
    13 function formatCurrency(v: number) {
    14   return '฿' + v.toLocaleString('th-TH', { minimumFractionDigits: 2, maximumFractionDigits: 2 });
    15 }
    16 
    17 function thaiDate(d: Date) {
    18   return d.toLocaleDateString('th-TH', { day: 'numeric', month: 'short', year: 'numeric' });
    19 }
    20 
    21 function thaiTime(d: Date) {
    22   return d.toLocaleTimeString('th-TH', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });
    23 }
    24 
    25 function dateRange(daysBack: number): { start: string; end: string; label: string } {
    26   const now = new Date();
    27   const start = new Date(now);
    28   start.setDate(now.getDate() - daysBack);
    29   start.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
    30   const end = new Date(now);
    31   end.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);
    32   const label = daysBack === 0 ? 'วันนี้' : daysBack === 1 ? 'เมื่อวาน' : `${daysBack + 1} วันล่าสุด`;
    33   return { start: start.toISOString(), end: end.toISOString(), label };
    34 }
    35 
    36 // ─── ASCII mini bar chart helper ───────────────────────────────────────────
    37 function asciiBar(value: number, max: number, width = 12): string {
    38   if (max === 0) return '░'.repeat(width);
    39   const filled = Math.round((value / max) * width);
    40   return '█'.repeat(filled) + '░'.repeat(width - filled);
    41 }
    42 
    43 // -------- Query daily report --------
    44 async function getDailyReport(
    45   supabase: ReturnType<typeof createClient>,
    46   storeId: string,
    47   daysBack: number,
    48 ): Promise<string> {
    49   const { start, end, label } = dateRange(daysBack);
    50 
    51   const { data: txData } = await supabase
    52     .from('transactions')
    53     .select('total, payment_method, items:transaction_items(unit_price, cost, quantity, product_name)')
    54     .eq('store_id', storeId)
    55     .eq('status', 'completed')
    56     .gte('created_at', start)
    57     .lte('created_at', end);
    58 
    59   const txArr = Array.isArray(txData) ? txData : [];
    60   const totalSales = txArr.reduce((s: number, t: any) => s + (t.total || 0), 0);
    61   const totalOrders = txArr.length;
    62   const totalProfit = txArr.reduce((s: number, t: any) => {
    63     const items = Array.isArray(t.items) ? t.items : [];
    64     return s + items.reduce((si: number, i: any) => si + ((i.unit_price - i.cost) * i.quantity), 0);
    65   }, 0);
    66   const profitMargin = totalSales > 0 ? ((totalProfit / totalSales) * 100).toFixed(1) : '0.0';
    67   const avgOrder = totalOrders > 0 ? totalSales / totalOrders : 0;
    68 
    69   // Payment method breakdown
    70   const payMap: Record<string, number> = {};
    71   txArr.forEach((t: any) => { payMap[t.payment_method] = (payMap[t.payment_method] || 0) + (t.total || 0); });
    72   const payLabels: Record<string, string> = { cash: '💵 เงินสด', card: '💳 บัตร', qr: '📱 QR' };
    73 
    74   // Top 3 products
    75   const productMap: Record<string, { qty: number; revenue: number }> = {};
    76   txArr.forEach((t: any) => {
    77     (Array.isArray(t.items) ? t.items : []).forEach((i: any) => {
    78       if (!productMap[i.product_name]) productMap[i.product_name] = { qty: 0, revenue: 0 };
    79       productMap[i.product_name].qty += i.quantity;
    80       productMap[i.product_name].revenue += i.unit_price * i.quantity;
    81     });
    82   });
    83   const topProducts = Object.entries(productMap).sort((a, b) => b[1].qty - a[1].qty).slice(0, 3);
    84 
    85   const dateLabel = daysBack === 1 ? thaiDate(new Date(Date.now() - 86400000)) : thaiDate(new Date());
    86 
    87   let msg = `📊 *รายงาน${label}* — ${dateLabel}\n${'─'.repeat(28)}\n`;
    88   msg += `💰 ยอดขาย: *${formatCurrency(totalSales)}*\n`;
    89   msg += `🛒 ออเดอร์: *${totalOrders} รายการ*\n`;
    90   msg += `📈 กำไร: *${formatCurrency(totalProfit)}* (${profitMargin}%)\n`;
    91   msg += `💳 เฉลี่ย/ออเดอร์: *${formatCurrency(avgOrder)}*\n`;
    92 
    93   if (Object.keys(payMap).length > 0) {
    94     msg += `${'─'.repeat(28)}\n💳 *ช่องทางชำระเงิน*\n`;
    95     Object.entries(payMap).forEach(([method, amount]) => {
    96       const pct = totalSales > 0 ? ((amount / totalSales) * 100).toFixed(0) : '0';
    97       msg += `${payLabels[method] ?? method}: ${formatCurrency(amount)} (${pct}%)\n`;
    98     });
    99   }
   100 
   101   if (topProducts.length > 0) {
   102     msg += `${'─'.repeat(28)}\n🏆 *สินค้าขายดี*\n`;
   103     topProducts.forEach(([name, d], i) => {
   104       msg += `${i + 1}. ${name} — ${d.qty} ชิ้น\n`;
   105     });
   106   }
   107   return msg;
   108 }

   110 // -------- Weekly chart --------
   111 async function getWeekReport(
   112   supabase: ReturnType<typeof createClient>,
   113   storeId: string,
   114 ): Promise<string> {
   115   const lines: { day: string; sales: number; orders: number }[] = [];
   116   for (let i = 6; i >= 0; i--) {
   117     const { start, end } = dateRange(i);
   118     const { data } = await supabase
   119       .from('transactions')
   120       .select('total')
   121       .eq('store_id', storeId)
   122       .eq('status', 'completed')
   123       .gte('created_at', start)
   124       .lte('created_at', end);
   125     const arr = Array.isArray(data) ? data : [];
   126     const sales = arr.reduce((s: number, t: any) => s + (t.total || 0), 0);
   127     const d = new Date(); d.setDate(d.getDate() - i);
   128     lines.push({ day: thaiDate(d), sales, orders: arr.length });
   129   }
   130   const maxSales = Math.max(...lines.map(l => l.sales), 1);
   131   let weekTotal = lines.reduce((s, l) => s + l.sales, 0);
   132 
   133   let msg = `📈 *ยอดขาย 7 วันล่าสุด*\n${'─'.repeat(28)}\n`;
   134   lines.forEach((l, i) => {
   135     const bar = asciiBar(l.sales, maxSales, 10);
   136     const isToday = i === lines.length - 1;
   137     msg += `${isToday ? '📍' : '  '} ${l.day}\n`;
   138     msg += `   ${bar} *${formatCurrency(l.sales)}* (${l.orders} ออเดอร์)\n`;
   139   });
   140   msg += `${'─'.repeat(28)}\n💰 รวม 7 วัน: *${formatCurrency(weekTotal)}*\n`;
   141   return msg;
   142 }

   144 // -------- Low stock --------
   145 async function getLowStock(
   146   supabase: ReturnType<typeof createClient>,
   147   storeId: string,
   148 ): Promise<string> {
   149   const { data: settings } = await supabase
   150     .from('store_settings').select('low_stock_threshold').eq('store_id', storeId).maybeSingle();
   151   const threshold = settings?.low_stock_threshold ?? 10;
   152 
   153   const { data: products } = await supabase
   154     .from('products').select('name, stock')
   155     .eq('store_id', storeId).eq('is_active', true)
   156     .lte('stock', threshold).order('stock', { ascending: true }).limit(15);
   157 
   158   const arr = Array.isArray(products) ? products : [];
   159   if (arr.length === 0) return `✅ *สต็อกสินค้า*\n\nทุกรายการมีสต็อกเพียงพอ (เกณฑ์ ${threshold} ชิ้น)`;
   160 
   161   const maxStock = Math.max(...arr.map((p: any) => p.stock), threshold);
   162   let msg = `📦 *สินค้าสต็อกต่ำ* (≤${threshold} ชิ้น)\n${'─'.repeat(28)}\n`;
   163   arr.forEach((p: any) => {
   164     const icon = p.stock === 0 ? '🔴' : p.stock <= 3 ? '🟠' : '🟡';
   165     const bar = asciiBar(p.stock, maxStock, 8);
   166     msg += `${icon} *${p.name}*\n   ${bar} ${p.stock} ชิ้น\n`;
   167   });
   168   return msg;
   169 }

   171 // -------- Recent fraud alerts --------
   172 async function getRecentFraud(

   174   storeId: string,

   184   const sevIcon: Record<string, string> = { critical: '🚨', high: '🔴', medium: '🟠', low: '🟡' };

   186   arr.forEach((a: any) => {
   187     msg += `${sevIcon[a.severity] ?? '⚠️'} *${a.username}* [${thaiTime(new Date(a.created_at))}]\n${a.description}\n\n`;
   188   });
   189   return msg;

   192 // -------- Cashiers on duty today --------
   193 async function getCashiersToday(
   194   supabase: ReturnType<typeof createClient>,
   195   storeId: string,
   196 ): Promise<string> {
   197   const { start, end } = dateRange(0);
   198 
   199   // Get distinct users who sold today
   200   const { data: txData } = await supabase
   201     .from('transactions')
   202     .select('cashier_id, cashier_name, total, status')
   203     .eq('store_id', storeId)
   204     .gte('created_at', start)
   205     .lte('created_at', end);
   206 
   207   const arr = Array.isArray(txData) ? txData : [];
   208   const cashierMap: Record<string, { name: string; sales: number; orders: number; voids: number }> = {};
   209   arr.forEach((t: any) => {
   210     const id = t.cashier_id || t.cashier_name || 'unknown';
   211     if (!cashierMap[id]) cashierMap[id] = { name: t.cashier_name || id, sales: 0, orders: 0, voids: 0 };
   212     if (t.status === 'completed') { cashierMap[id].sales += t.total || 0; cashierMap[id].orders++; }
   213     if (t.status === 'voided') cashierMap[id].voids++;
   214   });
   215 
   216   const cashiers = Object.values(cashierMap).sort((a, b) => b.sales - a.sales);
   217   if (cashiers.length === 0) return `👥 *พนักงานวันนี้*\n\nยังไม่มีการขาย`;
   218 
   219   let msg = `👥 *พนักงานวันนี้* (${thaiDate(new Date())})\n${'─'.repeat(28)}\n`;
   220   cashiers.forEach((c, i) => {
   221     msg += `${i + 1}. *${c.name}*\n`;
   222     msg += `   💰 ${formatCurrency(c.sales)} | 🛒 ${c.orders} ออเดอร์`;
   223     if (c.voids > 0) msg += ` | ❌ ยกเลิก ${c.voids}`;
   224     msg += '\n';
   225   });
   226   return msg;
   227 }

   229 // -------- Void transactions today --------
   230 async function getVoidsToday(
   231   supabase: ReturnType<typeof createClient>,
   232   storeId: string,
   233 ): Promise<string> {
   234   const { start, end } = dateRange(0);
   235 
   236   const { data } = await supabase
   237     .from('transactions')
   238     .select('order_number, total, cashier_name, void_reason, updated_at')
   239     .eq('store_id', storeId)
   240     .eq('status', 'voided')
   241     .gte('created_at', start)
   242     .lte('created_at', end)
   243     .order('updated_at', { ascending: false });
   244 
   245   const arr = Array.isArray(data) ? data : [];
   246   const totalVoided = arr.reduce((s: number, t: any) => s + (t.total || 0), 0);
   247 
   248   if (arr.length === 0) return `✅ *การยกเลิกบิลวันนี้*\n\nไม่มีการยกเลิกบิลวันนี้`;
   249   let msg = `❌ *การยกเลิกบิลวันนี้* (${arr.length} รายการ)\n${'─'.repeat(28)}\n`;
   250   msg += `💸 รวมมูลค่าที่ยกเลิก: *${formatCurrency(totalVoided)}*\n${'─'.repeat(28)}\n`;
   251   arr.slice(0, 8).forEach((t: any) => {
   252     msg += `📋 *${t.order_number}* — ${formatCurrency(t.total)}\n`;
   253     msg += `   👤 ${t.cashier_name || 'ไม่ระบุ'} | ${thaiTime(new Date(t.updated_at))}\n`;
   254     if (t.void_reason) msg += `   📝 ${t.void_reason}\n`;
   255   });
   256   if (arr.length > 8) msg += `_...และอีก ${arr.length - 8} รายการ_\n`;
   257   return msg;
   258 }

   260 // -------- Quick summary --------
   261 async function getQuickSummary(
   262   supabase: ReturnType<typeof createClient>,
   263   storeId: string,
   264   storeName: string,
   265 ): Promise<string> {
   266   const { start: ts, end: te } = dateRange(0);
   267 
   268   const [txRes, fraudRes, lowRes, settingsRes] = await Promise.all([
   269     supabase.from('transactions').select('total, status').eq('store_id', storeId)
   270       .gte('created_at', ts).lte('created_at', te),
   271     supabase.from('fraud_alerts').select('id').eq('store_id', storeId).eq('is_reviewed', false),
   272     supabase.from('store_settings').select('low_stock_threshold').eq('store_id', storeId).maybeSingle(),
   273     supabase.from('products').select('stock').eq('store_id', storeId).eq('is_active', true),
   274   ]);
   275 
   276   const txArr = Array.isArray(txRes.data) ? txRes.data : [];
   277   const threshold = lowRes.data?.low_stock_threshold ?? 10;
   278   const allProducts = Array.isArray(settingsRes.data) ? settingsRes.data : (Array.isArray(txRes.data) ? [] : []);
   279   const prodArr = Array.isArray(settingsRes.data) ? [] : (Array.isArray(txRes.data) ? [] : []);
   280 
   281   const completedTx = txArr.filter((t: any) => t.status === 'completed');
   282   const voidedCount = txArr.filter((t: any) => t.status === 'voided').length;
   283   const totalSales = completedTx.reduce((s: number, t: any) => s + (t.total || 0), 0);
   284   const fraudCount = Array.isArray(fraudRes.data) ? fraudRes.data.length : 0;
   285 
   286   const now = new Date();
   287   let msg = `🏪 *${storeName}*\n`;
   288   msg += `📍 สรุปด่วน — ${thaiDate(now)} ${thaiTime(now)}\n`;
   289   msg += `${'═'.repeat(28)}\n`;
   290   msg += `💰 ยอดขาย: *${formatCurrency(totalSales)}*\n`;
   291   msg += `🛒 ออเดอร์: *${completedTx.length}* รายการ\n`;
   292   if (voidedCount > 0) msg += `❌ ยกเลิก: *${voidedCount}* บิล\n`;
   293   if (fraudCount > 0) msg += `🚨 แจ้งเตือน: *${fraudCount}* รายการ ⚠️\n`;
   294   msg += `\n_อัปเดต ${thaiTime(now)}_`;
   295   return msg;
   296 }

   321 // -------- Send reply --------
   322 async function sendReply(
   323   botToken: string,
   324   chatId: number | string,
   325   text: string,
   326   withMenu = true,
   327 ) {
   328   const payload: Record<string, unknown> = { chat_id: chatId, text, parse_mode: 'Markdown' };
   329   if (withMenu) payload.reply_markup = buildKeyboard();
   330   await fetch(`https://api.telegram.org/bot${botToken}/sendMessage`, {
   331     method: 'POST',
   332     headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
   333     body: JSON.stringify(payload),
   334   });
   335 }
   336 
   337 async function answerCallback(botToken: string, callbackQueryId: string, text?: string) {
   338   await fetch(`https://api.telegram.org/bot${botToken}/answerCallbackQuery`, {
   339     method: 'POST',
   340     headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
   341     body: JSON.stringify({ callback_query_id: callbackQueryId, text: text ?? '' }),
   342   });
   343 }

   345 // -------- Main handler --------
   346 serve(async (req) => {
   347   if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') return new Response('ok', { headers: corsHeaders });
   348   if (req.method === 'GET') {
   349     return new Response(JSON.stringify({ ok: true, service: 'telegram-webhook' }), {
   350       headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
   351     });
   352   }
   353 
   354   try {
   355     const update = await req.json();
   356     const supabase = createClient(SUPABASE_URL, SUPABASE_SERVICE_KEY);
   357 
   358     const message = update.message;
   359     const callbackQuery = update.callback_query;
   360     const chatId: number = message?.chat?.id ?? callbackQuery?.message?.chat?.id;
   361     if (!chatId) return new Response(JSON.stringify({ ok: true }), { headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } });
   362 
   363     const { data: settings } = await supabase
   364       .from('store_settings')
   365       .select('store_id, store_name, telegram_bot_token, telegram_chat_id')
   366       .eq('telegram_chat_id', String(chatId))
   367       .maybeSingle();
   368 
   369     if (!settings?.store_id || !settings?.telegram_bot_token) {
   370       return new Response(JSON.stringify({ ok: true }), { headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } });
   371     }
   372 
   373     const botToken = settings.telegram_bot_token;
   374     const storeId = settings.store_id;
   375     const storeName = settings.store_name || 'ร้านของฉัน';
   376 
   377     // Handler map for commands + callbacks
   378     const handlers: Record<string, () => Promise<string>> = {
   379       report_today: () => getDailyReport(supabase, storeId, 0),
   380       report_yesterday: () => getDailyReport(supabase, storeId, 1),
   381       report_week: () => getWeekReport(supabase, storeId),
   382       stock_low: () => getLowStock(supabase, storeId),
   383       fraud_recent: () => getRecentFraud(supabase, storeId),
   384       cashiers_today: () => getCashiersToday(supabase, storeId),
   385       voids_today: () => getVoidsToday(supabase, storeId),
   386       quick_summary: () => getQuickSummary(supabase, storeId, storeName),
   387       menu: async () => `🏠 *เมนูหลัก* — ${storeName}\n\nเลือกรายงานที่ต้องการ:`,
   388     };
   389 
   390     // Text commands
   391     if (message?.text) {
   392       const cmd = message.text.trim().toLowerCase().replace(/^\//, '');
   393       let replyText = '';
   394 
   395       const cmdMap: Record<string, string> = {
   396         start: 'menu', help: 'menu', menu: 'menu',
   397         today: 'report_today', yesterday: 'report_yesterday', week: 'report_week',
   398         stock: 'stock_low', alerts: 'fraud_recent',
   399         cashiers: 'cashiers_today', voids: 'voids_today', summary: 'quick_summary',
   400       };
   401 
   402       const handlerKey = cmdMap[cmd];
   403       if (handlerKey && handlers[handlerKey]) {
   404         if (handlerKey === 'menu') {
   405           replyText = `👋 *สวัสดี! POS Bot พร้อมให้บริการ*\n\n🏪 *${storeName}*\n\nเลือกจากเมนู หรือพิมพ์คำสั่ง:\n/today /yesterday /week /stock /alerts /cashiers /voids /summary`;
   406         } else {
   407           replyText = await handlers[handlerKey]();
   408         }
   409       } else {
   410         replyText = `ไม่เข้าใจคำสั่ง\nพิมพ์ /menu เพื่อดูเมนู`;
   411       }
   412       await sendReply(botToken, chatId, replyText, true);
   413     }
   414 
   415     // Callback query (inline button press)
   416     if (callbackQuery) {
   417       const data = callbackQuery.data as string;
   418       await answerCallback(botToken, callbackQuery.id, '⏳ กำลังโหลด...');
   419       const handler = handlers[data];
   420       const replyText = handler ? await handler() : 'ไม่รู้จักคำสั่งนี้';
   421       await sendReply(botToken, chatId, replyText, true);
   422     }
   423 
   424     return new Response(JSON.stringify({ ok: true }), {
   425       headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
   426     });
   427   } catch (err) {
   428     console.error('telegram-webhook error:', err);
   429     return new Response(JSON.stringify({ ok: true }), {
   430       headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
   431     });
   432   }
   433 });
   434 
   435 const corsHeaders = {
   436   'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
   437   'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'authorization, x-client-info, apikey, content-type',
   438 };
   439 
   440 const SUPABASE_URL = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_URL')!;
   441 const SUPABASE_SERVICE_KEY = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY')!;

   443 // -------- Helpers --------
   444 function formatCurrency(v: number) {
   445   return '฿' + v.toLocaleString('th-TH', { minimumFractionDigits: 2, maximumFractionDigits: 2 });
   446 }
   447 
   448 function thaiDate(d: Date) {
   449   return d.toLocaleDateString('th-TH', { day: 'numeric', month: 'short', year: 'numeric' });
   450 }
   451 
   452 function dateRange(daysBack: number): { start: string; end: string; label: string } {
   453   const now = new Date();
   454   const start = new Date(now);
   455   start.setDate(now.getDate() - daysBack);
   456   start.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
   457   const end = new Date(now);
   458   end.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);
   459   const label = daysBack === 0 ? 'วันนี้' : daysBack === 1 ? 'เมื่อวาน' : `${daysBack + 1} วันล่าสุด`;
   460   return { start: start.toISOString(), end: end.toISOString(), label };
   461 }

    31 // Convert base64 data-URL to Uint8Array
    32 function base64ToBytes(dataUrl: string): { bytes: Uint8Array; mime: string } {
    33   const [meta, b64] = dataUrl.split(',');
    34   const mime = meta.match(/:(.*?);/)?.[1] ?? 'image/png';
    35   const binary = atob(b64);
    36   const bytes = new Uint8Array(binary.length);
    37   for (let i = 0; i < binary.length; i++) bytes[i] = binary.charCodeAt(i);
    38   return { bytes, mime };
    39 }

   120         JSON.stringify({ success: false, error: result.description ?? 'Telegram API error' }),
   121         { status: 400, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } },
   122       );
   123     }
   124 
   125     return new Response(
   126       JSON.stringify({ success: true }),
   127       { headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } },
   128     );
   129   } catch (err) {
   130     return new Response(
   131       JSON.stringify({ success: false, error: String(err) }),
   132       { status: 500, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } },
   133     );
   134   }
   135 });

// ประเภทข้อมูลหลักของระบบ POS

export type UserRole = 'super_admin' | 'store_owner' | 'admin' | 'cashier';

// ============ Store (Multi-tenant) ============
export interface Store {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  address: string;
  phone: string;
  is_active: boolean;
  created_at: string;
  updated_at: string;
}

// ============ ระบบยศและสิทธิ์ ============
export type PermissionKey =
  | 'view_dashboard'
  | 'view_reports'
  | 'view_profit'
  | 'manage_products'
  | 'manage_inventory'
  | 'manage_users'
  | 'manage_settings'
  | 'process_sales'
  | 'void_transactions'
  | 'view_transactions'
  | 'view_all_transactions'
  | 'manage_categories'
  | 'view_cost'
  | 'manage_roles'
  | 'view_audit_log'
  | 'view_fraud_alerts'
  | 'issue_warnings';

export type Permissions = Partial<Record<PermissionKey, boolean>>;

export interface Role {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  color: string;
  is_system: boolean;
  permissions: Permissions;
  sort_order: number;
  created_at: string;
  updated_at: string;
}

// ============ Audit & Fraud ============
export type AuditSeverity = 'info' | 'warning' | 'critical';
export type FraudSeverity = 'low' | 'medium' | 'high';

export interface AuditLog {
  id: string;
  user_id: string | null;
  username: string | null;
  store_id: string | null;
  action: string;
  entity_type: string | null;
  entity_id: string | null;
  details: Record<string, unknown>;
  severity: AuditSeverity;
  ip_address: string | null;
  created_at: string;
}

export interface FraudAlert {
  id: string;
  user_id: string | null;
  username: string | null;
  store_id: string | null;
  alert_type: string;
  severity: FraudSeverity;
  description: string;
  details: Record<string, unknown>;
  is_reviewed: boolean;
  reviewed_by: string | null;
  reviewed_at: string | null;
  created_at: string;
}

export interface Profile {
  id: string;
  username: string;
  full_name: string | null;
  email: string | null;
  role: UserRole;
  role_id: string | null;
  store_id: string | null;
  is_active: boolean;
  warning_status: 'normal' | 'yellow_card' | 'red_card';
  created_at: string;
  updated_at: string;
  // joined
  custom_role?: Role | null;
}

export interface StoreSettings {
  id: string;
  store_name: string;
  address: string;
  phone: string;
  tax_rate: number;
  auto_print_receipt: boolean;
  low_stock_threshold: number;
  currency: string;
  telegram_bot_token: string | null;
  telegram_chat_id: string | null;
  max_void_per_day: number;
  logo_url: string | null;
  updated_at: string;
}

export interface WarningRecord {
  id: string;
  user_id: string;
  issued_by: string;
  warning_type: 'yellow_card' | 'red_card';
  reason: string;
  created_at: string;
  // joined

}

export interface SystemSetting {
  id: string;
  key: string;
  value: string | null;
  description: string | null;
  updated_at: string;
}

export interface Category {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  description: string;
  sort_order: number;
  created_at: string;
}

export interface Product {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  sku: string | null;
  barcode: string | null;
  category_id: string | null;
  price: number;
  cost: number;
  stock: number;
  image_url: string | null;
  is_active: boolean;
  created_at: string;

}

export type PaymentMethod = 'cash' | 'card' | 'qr';
export type TransactionStatus = 'completed' | 'voided' | 'refunded';

export interface Transaction {
  id: string;

  subtotal: number;

    48	  }
    49	  if (key === 'month') {

const settingsSchema = z.object({
  store_name: z.string().min(1, 'กรอกชื่อร้าน'),
  address: z.string().optional(),
  phone: z.string().optional(),
  tax_rate: z.coerce.number().min(0).max(100),
  auto_print_receipt: z.boolean(),
  low_stock_threshold: z.coerce.number().int().min(1),
  max_void_per_day: z.coerce.number().int().min(1).max(999),
});
type SettingsForm = z.infer<typeof settingsSchema>;

const telegramSchema = z.object({
  telegram_bot_token: z.string().optional(),
  telegram_chat_id: z.string().optional(),
});
type TelegramForm = z.infer<typeof telegramSchema>;

const catSchema = z.object({
  name: z.string().min(1, 'กรอกชื่อหมวดหมู่'),
  description: z.string().optional(),
  sort_order: z.coerce.number().int().min(0),
});
type CatForm = z.infer<typeof catSchema>;

const badgeSchema = z.object({
  name: z.string().min(1, 'กรอกชื่อ Badge'),
  color: z.string().min(4, 'เลือกสี'),
  emoji: z.string().min(1, 'กรอก Emoji'),
  description: z.string().optional(),
  sort_order: z.coerce.number().int().min(0),
});
type BadgeForm = z.infer<typeof badgeSchema>;

  });
  const catForm = useForm<CatForm>({
    resolver: zodResolver(catSchema),
    defaultValues: { name: '', description: '', sort_order: 0 },
  });
  const badgeForm = useForm<BadgeForm>({

    defaultValues: { name: '', color: '#6366f1', emoji: '🏷️', description: '', sort_order: 0 },

  const watchColor = badgeForm.watch('color');
  const watchEmoji = badgeForm.watch('emoji');
  const watchName = badgeForm.watch('name');

  useEffect(() => { loadSettings(); loadCategories(); loadBadges(); }, []);

  const loadSettings = async () => {
    setLoadingSettings(true);
    const { data } = await supabase.from('store_settings').select('*').maybeSingle();
    if (data) {
      const s = data as StoreSettings;
      setSettings(s);
      settingsForm.reset({
        store_name: s.store_name, address: s.address || '', phone: s.phone || '',
        tax_rate: s.tax_rate, auto_print_receipt: s.auto_print_receipt,
        low_stock_threshold: s.low_stock_threshold, max_void_per_day: s.max_void_per_day || 5,
      });
      telegramForm.reset({
        telegram_bot_token: s.telegram_bot_token || '',
        telegram_chat_id: s.telegram_chat_id || '',
      });
      if (s.telegram_bot_token && s.telegram_chat_id) setTelegramStatus('ok');
    }
    setLoadingSettings(false);
  };

  const loadCategories = async () => {
    setLoadingCats(true);
    const { data } = await supabase.from('categories').select('*').order('sort_order');
    setCategories(Array.isArray(data) ? data as Category[] : []);
    setLoadingCats(false);
  };

  const loadBadges = async () => {
    setLoadingBadges(true);
    const { data } = await supabase.from('store_roles').select('*').order('sort_order');
    setStoreRoles(Array.isArray(data) ? data as StoreRole[] : []);
    setLoadingBadges(false);
  };

  const onSaveSettings = async (data: SettingsForm) => {
    setSavingSettings(true);
    const payload = {
      store_name: data.store_name, address: data.address || '', phone: data.phone || '',
      tax_rate: data.tax_rate, auto_print_receipt: data.auto_print_receipt,
      low_stock_threshold: data.low_stock_threshold, max_void_per_day: data.max_void_per_day,
      updated_at: new Date().toISOString(), store_id: profile?.store_id ?? null,
    };
    const { error } = settings?.id
      ? await supabase.from('store_settings').update(payload).eq('id', settings.id)
      : await supabase.from('store_settings').insert(payload);
    setSavingSettings(false);
    if (error) { toast.error(t('common.error')); return; }
    toast.success(t('settings.saveSuccess'));
    loadSettings();
  };

  const onSaveTelegram = async (data: TelegramForm) => {
    if (!settings?.id) { toast.error(t('settings.saveFirst')); return; }
    setSavingTelegram(true);
    const { error } = await supabase.from('store_settings').update({
      telegram_bot_token: data.telegram_bot_token || null,
      telegram_chat_id: data.telegram_chat_id || null,
      updated_at: new Date().toISOString(),
    }).eq('id', settings.id);
    setSavingTelegram(false);
    if (error) { toast.error(t('common.error')); return; }
    toast.success(t('settings.saveSuccess'));
    setTelegramStatus(data.telegram_bot_token && data.telegram_chat_id ? 'ok' : 'idle');
    loadSettings();
  };

  const onTestTelegram = async () => {
    const { telegram_bot_token, telegram_chat_id } = telegramForm.getValues();

      toast.error(t('settings.enterTokenFirst')); return;

    const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke('send-telegram', {
      body: {
        bot_token: telegram_bot_token, chat_id: telegram_chat_id, with_menu: true,

export function AuthProvider({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) {

  const loadStore = useCallback(async (storeId: string | null | undefined) => {
    if (!storeId) { setStore(null); return; }
    const { data } = await supabase
      .from('stores')
      .select('*')
      .eq('id', storeId)
      .maybeSingle();
    setStore(data ?? null);
  }, []);

  const applyProfile = useCallback((p: Profile | null) => {
    setProfile(p);
    setPermissions(resolvePermissions(p));
    // โหลดร้านแบบ background (ไม่ await ที่นี่)
    if (p?.store_id && p.role !== 'super_admin') {
      loadStore(p.store_id);
    } else {

export default function DashboardPage() {
  const { t } = useTranslation();
  const [preset, setPreset] = useState<PresetKey>('today');

  const PRESETS: { key: PresetKey; label: string }[] = [
    { key: 'today', label: t('dashboard.today') },
    { key: 'yesterday', label: t('dashboard.yesterday') },
    { key: 'week', label: t('dashboard.last7days') },
    { key: 'month', label: t('dashboard.thisMonth') },
    { key: 'custom', label: t('dashboard.customRange') },
  ];
  const [customFrom, setCustomFrom] = useState(toDateStr(new Date()));
  const [customTo, setCustomTo] = useState(toDateStr(new Date()));
  const [showCustom, setShowCustom] = useState(false);

  const [stats, setStats] = useState<DashboardStats | null>(null);
  const [chartData, setChartData] = useState<ChartData[]>([]);
  const [recentTx, setRecentTx] = useState<Transaction[]>([]);
  const [lowStockProducts, setLowStockProducts] = useState<Product[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

  const getRange = useCallback(() => {
    if (preset === 'custom') return { from: customFrom, to: customTo };
    return getPresetRange(preset);
  }, [preset, customFrom, customTo]);

  const loadDashboard = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    const { from, to } = getRange();

    const [txRes, productsRes, settingsRes] = await Promise.all([
      supabase
        .from('transactions')
        .select('*, items:transaction_items(unit_price, cost, quantity, product_name)')
        .gte('created_at', `${from}T00:00:00`)
        .lte('created_at', `${to}T23:59:59`)
        .eq('status', 'completed')
        .order('created_at', { ascending: false }),
      supabase.from('products').select('*, category:categories(name)').eq('is_active', true),
      supabase.from('store_settings').select('low_stock_threshold').maybeSingle(),
    ]);

    const txArr = Array.isArray(txRes.data) ? txRes.data : [];
    const allProducts = Array.isArray(productsRes.data) ? productsRes.data : [];
    const threshold = settingsRes.data?.low_stock_threshold || 10;

    const totalSales = txArr.reduce((s: number, t: any) => s + (t.total || 0), 0);
    const totalProfit = txArr.reduce((s: number, t: any) => {
      const items = Array.isArray(t.items) ? t.items : [];
      return s + items.reduce((si: number, i: any) => si + ((i.unit_price - i.cost) * i.quantity), 0);
    }, 0);

    setStats({
      totalSales,
      totalOrders: txArr.length,
      totalProfit,
      lowStockCount: allProducts.filter((p: Product) => p.stock <= threshold).length,
    });
    setRecentTx(txArr.slice(0, 5) as Transaction[]);
    setLowStockProducts(allProducts.filter((p: Product) => p.stock <= threshold).slice(0, 5) as Product[]);

    // Build chart: one bar per day in range
    const start = new Date(`${from}T00:00:00`);
    const end = new Date(`${to}T00:00:00`);
    const days: ChartData[] = [];
    for (let d = new Date(start); d <= end; d.setDate(d.getDate() + 1)) {
      const ds = toDateStr(d);
      const dayTx = txArr.filter((t: any) => t.created_at?.startsWith(ds));
      const sales = dayTx.reduce((s: number, t: any) => s + (t.total || 0), 0);
      const profit = dayTx.reduce((s: number, t: any) => {
        const items = Array.isArray(t.items) ? t.items : [];
        return s + items.reduce((si: number, it: any) => si + ((it.unit_price - it.cost) * it.quantity), 0);
      }, 0);
      days.push({ label: formatDate(new Date(ds), 'short'), sales: Math.round(sales), profit: Math.round(profit) });
    }
    setChartData(days);
    setLoading(false);
  }, [getRange]);

  useEffect(() => { loadDashboard(); }, [loadDashboard]);

  const applyPreset = (key: PresetKey) => {
    setPreset(key);
    if (key === 'custom') { setShowCustom(true); return; }
    setShowCustom(false);
  };

  const activeLabel = preset === 'custom'
    ? `${customFrom} — ${customTo}`
    : PRESETS.find(p => p.key === preset)?.label ?? t('dashboard.today');

  const statCards = [
    { title: t('dashboard.totalSales'), value: stats ? formatCurrency(stats.totalSales) : '-', icon: DollarSign, color: 'text-primary', bg: 'bg-primary/10' },
    { title: t('dashboard.totalOrders'), value: stats ? `${stats.totalOrders} ${t('common.items')}` : '-', icon: ShoppingBag, color: 'text-info', bg: 'bg-info/10' },
    { title: t('dashboard.totalProfit'), value: stats ? formatCurrency(stats.totalProfit) : '-', icon: TrendingUp, color: 'text-success', bg: 'bg-success/10' },
    { title: t('dashboard.lowStock'), value: stats ? `${stats.lowStockCount} ${t('common.items')}` : '-', icon: AlertTriangle, color: 'text-warning', bg: 'bg-warning/10' },
  ];

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6" id="dashboard-capture">
      {/* Header + date range picker */}
      <div className="flex flex-col md:flex-row md:items-center gap-3">
        <div>
          <h2 className="text-xl font-bold text-foreground text-balance">{t('dashboard.title')}</h2>
          <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mt-0.5">{t('dashboard.subtitle')}</p>
        </div>
        <div className="md:ml-auto flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2">
          <Button
            variant="outline"
            size="sm"
            onClick={() => sendScreenshotToTelegram({ elementId: 'dashboard-capture', caption: `📊 ${t('dashboard.title')} — ${activeLabel}` })}
            title={t('dashboard.sendToTelegram')}
          >
            <Camera className="w-4 h-4 mr-1.5" />
            <span className="hidden md:inline">{t('dashboard.sendToTelegram')}</span>
          </Button>
          <DropdownMenu>
            <DropdownMenuTrigger asChild>
              <Button variant="outline" className="gap-2 min-w-0">
                <CalendarDays className="w-4 h-4 shrink-0" />
                <span className="truncate max-w-[180px]">{activeLabel}</span>
                <ChevronDown className="w-3.5 h-3.5 shrink-0" />
              </Button>
            </DropdownMenuTrigger>
            <DropdownMenuContent align="end" className="w-48">
              {PRESETS.filter(p => p.key !== 'custom').map(p => (
                <DropdownMenuItem key={p.key} onClick={() => applyPreset(p.key)}
                  className={preset === p.key ? 'bg-primary/10 text-primary font-medium' : ''}>
                  {p.label}
                </DropdownMenuItem>
              ))}
              <DropdownMenuSeparator />
              <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => applyPreset('custom')}
                className={preset === 'custom' ? 'bg-primary/10 text-primary font-medium' : ''}>
                {t('dashboard.customRange')}...
              </DropdownMenuItem>
            </DropdownMenuContent>
          </DropdownMenu>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Custom date range inputs */}
      {showCustom && (
        <div className="flex flex-wrap items-end gap-3 p-4 bg-muted/50 rounded-xl border border-border">
          <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
            <label className="text-xs text-muted-foreground font-medium">{t('common.from')}</label>
===REPORTS===
  useEffect(() => { loadReport(); }, [loadReport]);

     1 import { cn } from '@/lib/utils'
     2 import { type UseSupabaseUploadReturn } from '@/hooks/use-supabase-upload'
