     4 import { CheckCircle, File, Loader2, Upload, X } from 'lucide-react'
     5 import { createContext, type PropsWithChildren, useCallback, useContext } from 'react'
     6 
     7 export const formatBytes = (
     8   bytes: number,
     9   decimals = 2,
    10   size?: 'bytes' | 'KB' | 'MB' | 'GB' | 'TB' | 'PB' | 'EB' | 'ZB' | 'YB'
    11 ) => {
    12   const k = 1000
    13   const dm = decimals < 0 ? 0 : decimals
    14   const sizes = ['bytes', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB', 'TB', 'PB', 'EB', 'ZB', 'YB']
    15 
    16   if (bytes === 0 || bytes === undefined) return size !== undefined ? `0 ${size}` : '0 bytes'
    17   const i = size !== undefined ? sizes.indexOf(size) : Math.floor(Math.log(bytes) / Math.log(k))
    18   return parseFloat((bytes / Math.pow(k, i)).toFixed(dm)) + ' ' + sizes[i]
    19 }
    20 
    21 type DropzoneContextType = Omit<UseSupabaseUploadReturn, 'getRootProps' | 'getInputProps'>
    22 
    23 const DropzoneContext = createContext<DropzoneContextType | undefined>(undefined)
    24 
    25 type DropzoneProps = UseSupabaseUploadReturn & {
    26   className?: string
    27 }
    28 
    29 const Dropzone = ({
    30   className,
    31   children,
    32   getRootProps,
    33   getInputProps,
    34   ...restProps
    35 }: PropsWithChildren<DropzoneProps>) => {
    36   const isSuccess = restProps.isSuccess
    37   const isActive = restProps.isDragActive
    38   const isInvalid =
    39     (restProps.isDragActive && restProps.isDragReject) ||
    40     (restProps.errors.length > 0 && !restProps.isSuccess) ||
    41     restProps.files.some((file) => file.errors.length !== 0)
    42 
    43   return (
    44     <DropzoneContext.Provider value={{ ...restProps }}>
    45       <div
    46         {...getRootProps({
    47           className: cn(
    48             'border-2 border-gray-300 rounded-lg p-6 text-center bg-card transition-colors duration-300 text-foreground',
    49             className,
    50             isSuccess ? 'border-solid' : 'border-dashed',
    51             isActive && 'border-primary bg-primary/10',
    52             isInvalid && 'border-destructive bg-destructive/10'
    53           ),
    54         })}
    55       >
    56         <input {...getInputProps()} />
    57         {children}
    58       </div>
    59     </DropzoneContext.Provider>
    60   )
    61 }
    62 const DropzoneContent = ({ className }: { className?: string }) => {
    63   const {
    64     files,
    65     setFiles,
    66     onUpload,
    67     loading,
    68     successes,
    69     errors,
    70     maxFileSize,
    71     maxFiles,
    72     isSuccess,
    73   } = useDropzoneContext()
    74 
    75   const exceedMaxFiles = files.length > maxFiles
    76 
    77   const handleRemoveFile = useCallback(
    78     (fileName: string) => {
    79       setFiles(files.filter((file) => file.name !== fileName))
    80     },
    81     [files, setFiles]
    82   )
    83 
    84   if (isSuccess) {
    85     return (
    86       <div className={cn('flex flex-row items-center gap-x-2 justify-center', className)}>
    87         <CheckCircle size={16} className="text-primary" />
    88         <p className="text-primary text-sm">
    89           Successfully uploaded {files.length} file{files.length > 1 ? 's' : ''}
    90         </p>
    91       </div>
    92     )
    93   }
    94 
    95   return (
    96     <div className={cn('flex flex-col', className)}>
    97       {files.map((file, idx) => {
    98         const fileError = errors.find((e) => e.name === file.name)
    99         const isSuccessfullyUploaded = !!successes.find((e) => e === file.name)
   100 
   101         return (
   102           <div
   103             key={`${file.name}-${idx}`}
   104             className="flex items-center gap-x-4 border-b py-2 first:mt-4 last:mb-4 "
   105           >
   106             {file.type.startsWith('image/') ? (
   107               <div className="h-10 w-10 rounded border overflow-hidden shrink-0 bg-muted flex items-center justify-center">
   108                 <img src={file.preview} alt={file.name} className="object-cover" />
   109               </div>
   110             ) : (
   111               <div className="h-10 w-10 rounded border bg-muted flex items-center justify-center">
   112                 <File size={18} />
   113               </div>
   114             )}
   115 
   116             <div className="shrink grow flex flex-col items-start truncate">
   117               <p title={file.name} className="text-sm truncate max-w-full">
   118                 {file.name}
   119               </p>
   120               {file.errors.length > 0 ? (
   121                 <p className="text-xs text-destructive">
   122                   {file.errors
   123                     .map((e) =>
   124                       e.message.startsWith('File is larger than')
   125                         ? `File is larger than ${formatBytes(maxFileSize, 2)} (Size: ${formatBytes(file.size, 2)})`
   126                         : e.message
   127                     )
   128                     .join(', ')}
   129                 </p>
   130               ) : loading && !isSuccessfullyUploaded ? (
   131                 <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Uploading file...</p>
   132               ) : !!fileError ? (
   133                 <p className="text-xs text-destructive">Failed to upload: {fileError.message}</p>
   134               ) : isSuccessfullyUploaded ? (
   135                 <p className="text-xs text-primary">Successfully uploaded file</p>
   136               ) : (
   137                 <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{formatBytes(file.size, 2)}</p>
   138               )}
   139             </div>
   140 
   141             {!loading && !isSuccessfullyUploaded && (
   142               <Button
   143                 size="icon"
   144                 variant="link"
   145                 className="shrink-0 justify-self-end text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground"
   146                 onClick={() => handleRemoveFile(file.name)}
   147               >
   148                 <X />
   149               </Button>
   150             )}
   151           </div>
   152         )
   153       })}
   154       {exceedMaxFiles && (
   155         <p className="text-sm text-left mt-2 text-destructive">
   156           You may upload only up to {maxFiles} files, please remove {files.length - maxFiles} file
   157           {files.length - maxFiles > 1 ? 's' : ''}.
   158         </p>
   159       )}
   160       {files.length > 0 && !exceedMaxFiles && (
   161         <div className="mt-2">
   162           <Button
   163             variant="outline"
   164             onClick={onUpload}
   165             disabled={files.some((file) => file.errors.length !== 0) || loading}
   166           >
   167             {loading ? (
   168               <>
   169                 <Loader2 className="mr-2 h-4 w-4 animate-spin" />
   170                 Uploading...
   171               </>
   172             ) : (
   173               <>Upload files</>
   174             )}
   175           </Button>
   176         </div>
   177       )}
   178     </div>
   179   )
   180 }
   181 
   182 const DropzoneEmptyState = ({ className }: { className?: string }) => {
   183   const { maxFiles, maxFileSize, inputRef, isSuccess } = useDropzoneContext()
   184 
   185   if (isSuccess) {
   186     return null
   187   }
   188 
   189   return (
   190     <div className={cn('flex flex-col items-center gap-y-2', className)}>
   191       <Upload size={20} className="text-muted-foreground" />
   192       <p className="text-sm">
   193         Upload{!!maxFiles && maxFiles > 1 ? ` ${maxFiles}` : ''} file
   194         {!maxFiles || maxFiles > 1 ? 's' : ''}
   195       </p>
   196       <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-y-1">
   197         <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
   198           Drag and drop or{' '}
   199           <a
   200             onClick={() => inputRef.current?.click()}
   201             className="underline cursor-pointer transition hover:text-foreground"
   202           >
   203             select {maxFiles === 1 ? `file` : 'files'}
   204           </a>{' '}
   205           to upload
   206         </p>
   207         {maxFileSize !== Number.POSITIVE_INFINITY && (
   208           <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
   209             Maximum file size: {formatBytes(maxFileSize, 2)}
   210           </p>
   211         )}
   212       </div>
   213     </div>
   214   )
   215 }
   216 
   217 const useDropzoneContext = () => {
   218   const context = useContext(DropzoneContext)
   219 
   220   if (!context) {
   221     throw new Error('useDropzoneContext must be used within a Dropzone')
   222   }
   223 
   224   return context
   225 }
   226 
   227 export { Dropzone, DropzoneContent, DropzoneEmptyState, useDropzoneContext }
   228

SkillObservation(content='Base directory for this skill: /workspace/app-ca8n8duf25mp/.skills/supabase-server\n\n# Supabase Backend\n\nApplies to all frontend stacks (Web / MiniProgram / App). Covers Supabase server-side Schema, RLS, Edge Functions, Storage, Realtime, and Auth configuration.\n\n## Initial Setup\n\n- Use `supabase_init` to initialize the database or start it from a paused state\n\n## Schema Design\n\n- Minimize tables and columns; merge functionalities into single tables when possible\n- Set database-level default values for required fields\n  - Example: `owner_id uuid not null default auth.uid()`\n  - Example: `order_number text UNIQUE NOT NULL` — use a trigger bound to insert logic to auto-generate the order number\n- For multi-table relations, define them clearly to avoid missing link fields\n- ENUM values require explicit casts\n- **NEVER interact with `supabase/migrations/` directory** (including ls, cat, view)\n- Always apply changes through incremental migrations\n- Verify database state by querying table structure using `supabase_execute_sql`\n- Try to combine tasks and execute all SQL in a single run\n- Always consider performance and speed optimization\n- Disallow SQL statements with silent or ambiguous success semantics (e.g., `IF NOT EXISTS`, `IF EXISTS`) — all operations must fail explicitly when schema or data deviates from expectations\n\n## Data Insertion\n\n**Must-Add:**\n- System-required data (e.g., categories, form dropdown options)\n- **For image URLs**: Use `image_search` to get real URLs — **NEVER** use placeholder URLs like `https://placeholder-image.jpg`\n- Add initial seed data (INSERT INTO) in the migration SQL, using `image_search` for real image URLs\n\n**Allowed:**\n- Homepage display data (e.g., showcases, course previews, products)\n- Demo data (e.g., sample exam sets)\n\n**Forbidden:**\n- User data\n- User activity history (e.g., lottery, orders)\n- Real personal names or any privacy-related info\n\n## SQL Modification\n\n- If you have full context in memory, prioritize using it directly\n- If unsure about current data structure, query it first; do not rely on migration files\n- Under no circumstances should you view or modify migration files\n- If frontend requires a feature without a corresponding table, policy, or edge function, you may add it afterward\n- When modifying business data (non-DDL, policy, RPC, etc.), use `supabase_execute_sql`\n- Before writing api.ts, read the corresponding `supabase/migrations/*.sql` to confirm NOT NULL constraints for every column — context compression may lose field details; migrations are the ground truth\n\n## Security Policies (RLS)\n\n### Design Principles\n\n- **Every table MUST have RLS enabled** — no exceptions, regardless of whether login auth exists\n- **Full coverage per table**: Explicitly define policies for every combination of SELECT/INSERT/UPDATE/DELETE × {anon, authenticated, admin}. **Never leave any blank** — missing policies silently return empty data or 0 affected rows\n  - Per-table review checklist: anon × {S/I/U/D}, authenticated × {S/I/U/D}, admin × {S/I/U/D}\n  - Anticipate future features: add corresponding constraints now for role×operation combinations that may be needed later\n- **INSERT always requires a matching SELECT**: Any role granted INSERT permission MUST also have a SELECT policy defined\n  - Example: If a policy "allows anyone to submit", add one so "submitters can view their own submissions"\n- Frontend and backend permissions must be aligned\n  - No permission, no interaction\n  - All submit-capable forms must have explicit, role-based permissions\n- PostgREST silently returns 0 affected rows (no error) when UPDATE/DELETE does not match RLS — writes appear to succeed but nothing changed. Tables the frontend needs to mutate must have explicit UPDATE/DELETE policies defined\n- Clear role boundaries\n  - Admins must have full read/write access\n  - Roles must have complete and secure permissions defined for every possible interaction scenario\n- All internal checks must use `SECURITY DEFINER`\n\n### Implementation Notes\n\n- RLS should only depend on **static columns or secure functions**\n- **Policy self-loop**: A policy\'s USING clause must not query the same table it protects — use a `SECURITY DEFINER` helper function instead (it bypasses RLS when querying the table)\n- Use public views to expose read-only access to selected fields of high-privilege tables\n\n## Storage Buckets\n\n- Create for image/file uploads only\n- **CRITICAL**: NEVER store images/videos as Base64 in database\n- ALL image/video assets MUST be uploaded to Supabase Storage\n- When third-party APIs return image/video URLs, transfer to Storage in Edge Function\n- buckets must be created in migration SQL via `supabase_apply_migration` — **do not** create them dynamically inside Edge Functions\n- Frontend validation: 1MB limit, snake_case filenames\n\n\n## Edge Functions\n\n### When to Use\n\n- **MANDATORY for third-party API calls**: ALL external API integrations (payment, weather, maps, etc.) MUST be implemented through Edge Functions\n- **STRICTLY FORBIDDEN**: Direct third-party API calls from client-side code (fetch/axios in frontend components)\n- Server-side secrets and service-role operations\n- Sensitive payment logic requiring secure environment\n\n### Authoring\n\n- Create files under `supabase/functions/<function_name>/`\n- **CRITICAL**: Use `supabase_deploy_edge_function` to deploy after modifying or creating Edge Function files\n- Put cross-domain content in the `_shared/` directory\n- No URL imports — only npm and JSR\n- Do not add secrets unless explicitly required by API documentation\n- Handle CORS properly\n- `supabase.sql` forbidden in Edge Functions\n- `supabase.raw` forbidden in Edge Functions — use `.rpc()` for atomic operations\n- Response Content-Type must be chosen only from: `[\'application/json\', \'application/octet-stream\', \'text/event-stream\', \'multipart/form-data\']`\n- Make proper use of optimistic locking to ensure that subsequent settlement operations in the state flow are executed only once, even if called multiple times\n\n\n## Supabase Auth\n\n- Your knowledge may be outdated. **MUST** call `skill_action(skill="login")` to refresh with the latest information\n- Any form of third-party login (OAuth or SSO) must use the login skill as the knowledge basis\n\n## Supabase Realtime (low-frequency feature)\n\nWhen realtime capability is genuinely needed, read `references/realtime.md` — it covers server-side publication switches, per-stack client subscription patterns, and RN/weapp limitations.\n\n**Multi-identity scenarios**: Identity selection / role assignment logic **must NOT** be placed      1 import { createContext, useContext, useEffect, useState, useCallback, type ReactNode } from 'react';
     2 import { supabase } from '@/db/supabase';
     3 import type { User } from '@supabase/supabase-js';
     4 import type { PermissionKey, Permissions, Profile, Store } from '@/types/types';
     5 
     6 export async function getProfile(userId: string): Promise<Profile | null> {
     7   const { data, error } = await supabase
     8     .from('profiles')
     9     .select('*, custom_role:roles(*)')
    10     .eq('id', userId)
    11     .maybeSingle();
    12   if (error) {
    13     console.error('ดึงข้อมูลผู้ใช้ไม่สำเร็จ:', error);
    14     return null;
    15   }
    16   return data;
    17 }
    18 
    19 interface AuthContextType {
    20   user: User | null;
    21   profile: Profile | null;
    22   store: Store | null;
    23   permissions: Permissions;
    24   loading: boolean;
    25   isAdmin: boolean;
    26   isStoreOwner: boolean;
    27   isSuperAdmin: boolean;
    28   can: (permission: PermissionKey) => boolean;
    29   signInWithUsername: (username: string, password: string) => Promise<{ error: Error | null; blocked?: boolean; storeClosed?: boolean }>;
    30   signUpWithUsername: (username: string, password: string, fullName?: string, storeId?: string, role?: string) => Promise<{ error: Error | null }>;
    31   signOut: () => Promise<void>;
    32   refreshProfile: () => Promise<void>;
    33 }
    34 
    35 const AuthContext = createContext<AuthContextType | undefined>(undefined);
    36 
    37 /** รวม permissions จาก custom_role (ถ้ามี) หรือใช้ค่า default ตาม role */
    38 function resolvePermissions(profile: Profile | null): Permissions {
    39   if (!profile) return {};
    40   const allKeys: PermissionKey[] = [
    41     'view_dashboard','view_reports','view_profit','manage_products','manage_inventory',
    42     'manage_users','manage_settings','process_sales','void_transactions','view_transactions',
    43     'view_all_transactions','manage_categories','view_cost','manage_roles',
    44     'view_audit_log','view_fraud_alerts','issue_warnings',
    45   ];
    46   // super_admin + store_owner + admin มีสิทธิ์ทุกอย่าง
    47   if (['super_admin','store_owner','admin'].includes(profile.role)) {
    48     const all: Permissions = {};
    49     allKeys.forEach(k => { all[k] = true; });
    50     return all;
    51   }
    52   if (profile.custom_role?.permissions) return profile.custom_role.permissions;
    53   return { process_sales: true, view_transactions: true };
    54 }
    55 
    56 export function AuthProvider({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) {
    57   const [user, setUser] = useState<User | null>(null);
    58   const [profile, setProfile] = useState<Profile | null>(null);
    59   const [store, setStore] = useState<Store | null>(null);
    60   const [permissions, setPermissions] = useState<Permissions>({});
    61   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
    62 
    63   /** โหลดข้อมูลร้านใน background — ไม่บล็อก loading */
    64   const loadStore = useCallback(async (storeId: string | null | undefined) => {
    65     if (!storeId) { setStore(null); return; }
    66     const { data } = await supabase
    67       .from('stores')
    68       .select('*')
    69       .eq('id', storeId)
    70       .maybeSingle();
    71     setStore(data ?? null);
    72   }, []);
    73 
    74   const applyProfile = useCallback((p: Profile | null) => {
    75     setProfile(p);
    76     setPermissions(resolvePermissions(p));
    77     // โหลดร้านแบบ background (ไม่ await ที่นี่)
    78     if (p?.store_id && p.role !== 'super_admin') {
    79       loadStore(p.store_id);
    80     } else {
    81       setStore(null);
    82     }
    83   }, [loadStore]);
    84 
    85   const refreshProfile = useCallback(async () => {
    86     if (!user) { applyProfile(null); return; }
    87     const profileData = await getProfile(user.id);
    88     applyProfile(profileData);
    89   }, [user, applyProfile]);
    90 
    91   useEffect(() => {
    92     // ใช้ onAuthStateChange เป็น single source of truth สำหรับ session ครั้งแรก
    93     // SIGNED_IN จะถูกจัดการใน signInWithUsername โดยตรงเพื่อป้องกัน race condition
    94     const { data: { subscription } } = supabase.auth.onAuthStateChange(async (event, session) => {
    95       if (event === 'SIGNED_OUT') {
    96         // logout หรือ token หมดอายุ — ล้าง state กลับหน้า login
    97         setUser(null);
    98         applyProfile(null);
    99         setLoading(false);
   100         return;
   101       }
   102       if (event === 'INITIAL_SESSION') {
   103         // โหลด session ครั้งแรกตอนเปิดแอป
   104         if (session?.user) {
   105           setUser(session.user);
   106           const p = await getProfile(session.user.id);
   107           applyProfile(p);
   108         } else {
   109           setUser(null);
   110           applyProfile(null);
   111         }
   112         setLoading(false);
   113         return;
   114       }
   115       if (event === 'TOKEN_REFRESHED' && session?.user) {
   116         // token ต่ออายุสำเร็จ — อัปเดต user object ใหม่
   117         setUser(session.user);
   118       }
   119     });
   120 
   121     // fallback: ถ้า INITIAL_SESSION ไม่ยิงภายใน 5 วินาที ให้ยกเลิก loading
   122     const fallback = setTimeout(() => setLoading(false), 5000);
   123 
   124     return () => {
   125       subscription.unsubscribe();
   126       clearTimeout(fallback);
   127     };
   128   }, [applyProfile]);
   129 
   130   const signInWithUsername = async (username: string, password: string) => {
   131     try {
   132       const email = `${username}@miaoda.com`;
   133       const { data: { session }, error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({ email, password });
   134       if (error) throw error;
   135 
   136       // ดึงข้อมูลโปรไฟล์พร้อม store_id
   137       const { data: profileData } = await supabase
   138         .from('profiles')
   139         .select('*, custom_role:roles(*), warning_status, role, store_id')
   140         .eq('username', username)
   141         .maybeSingle();
   142 
   143       // บล็อคใบแดง
   144       if (profileData?.warning_status === 'red_card') {
   145         await supabase.auth.signOut();
   146         setUser(null);
   147         applyProfile(null);
   148         return { error: new Error('ACCOUNT_SUSPENDED'), blocked: true };
   149       }
   150 
   151       // ตรวจสอบว่าร้านยังเปิดอยู่ (เฉพาะ non-super_admin)
   152       if (profileData?.role !== 'super_admin' && profileData?.store_id) {
   153         const { data: storeData } = await supabase
   154           .from('stores')
   155           .select('is_active')
   156           .eq('id', profileData.store_id)
   157           .maybeSingle();
   158         if (storeData && !storeData.is_active) {
   159           await supabase.auth.signOut();
   160           setUser(null);
   161           applyProfile(null);
   162           return { error: new Error('STORE_CLOSED'), storeClosed: true };
   163         }
   164       }
   165 
   166       // ✅ อัปเดต state ทันทีก่อน return — ป้องกัน race condition กับ navigate('/')
   167       // onAuthStateChange(SIGNED_IN) จะยิงทีหลัง แต่ค่าจะเหมือนกัน
   168       if (session?.user) {
   169         setUser(session.user);
   170         applyProfile(profileData as Profile | null);
   171         setLoading(false);
   172       }
   173 
   174       return { error: null };
   175     } catch (error) {
   176       return { error: error as Error };
   177     }
   178   };
   179 
   180   const signUpWithUsername = async (
   181     username: string,
   182     password: string,
   183     fullName?: string,
   184     storeId?: string,
   185     role: string = 'cashier',
   186   ) => {
   187     try {
   188       const email = `${username}@miaoda.com`;
   189       const { error } = await supabase.auth.signUp({
   190         email,
   191         password,
   192         options: { data: { username, full_name: fullName || username, store_id: storeId, role } },
   193       });
   194       if (error) throw error;
   195       return { error: null };
   196     } catch (error) {
   197       return { error: error as Error };
   198     }
   199   };
   200 
   201   const signOut = async () => {
   202     await supabase.auth.signOut();
   203     setUser(null);
   204     await applyProfile(null);
   205   };
   206 
   207   const isAdmin = ['admin','store_owner','super_admin'].includes(profile?.role ?? '');
   208   const isStoreOwner = profile?.role === 'store_owner' || profile?.role === 'admin';
   209   const isSuperAdmin = profile?.role === 'super_admin';
   210 
   211   const can = useCallback((permission: PermissionKey): boolean => {
   212     if (isAdmin) return true;
   213     return permissions[permission] === true;
   214   }, [isAdmin, permissions]);
   215 
   216   return (
   217     <AuthContext.Provider value={{
   218       user, profile, store, permissions, loading,
   219       isAdmin, isStoreOwner, isSuperAdmin,
   220       can, signInWithUsername, signUpWithUsername, signOut, refreshProfile,
   221     }}>
   222       {children}
   223     </AuthContext.Provider>
   224   );
   225 }
   226 
   227 export function useAuth() {
   228   const context = useContext(AuthContext);
   229   if (context === undefined) {
   230     // Return safe defaults during HMR / Fast Refresh re-evaluation
   231     // instead of throwing — prevents crash when component is briefly
   232     // rendered outside the provider tree during hot reload.
   233     return {
   234       user: null, profile: null, store: null, permissions: {},
   235       loading: true, isAdmin: false, isStoreOwner: false, isSuperAdmin: false,
   236       can: () => false,
   237       signInWithUsername: async () => ({ error: new Error('No AuthProvider') }),
   238       signUpWithUsername: async () => ({ error: new Error('No AuthProvider') }),
   239       signOut: async () => {},
   240       refreshProfile: async () => {},
   241     } as AuthContextType;
   242   }
   243   return context;
   244 }
   245
